href="https://www.washingtonpost.com/politics/trump-impeachment-inquiry-live-updates/2019/10/04/9ff6d4a0-e627-11e9-a331-2df12d56a80b_story.html?tid=lk_interstitial_manual_1">Read the latest here</a></p></div><div><p class="font--body font-copy color-gray-darkest ma-0 pad-bottom-md undefined">President Trump ordered the removal of the U.S. ambassador to Ukraine over concerns that she was biased against him and an obstacle in his effort to get Ukrainians to investigate former vice president Joe Biden and his son Hunter.</p></div><div><p class="font--body font-copy color-gray-darkest ma-0 pad-bottom-md undefined">The Wall Street Journal <a href="https://www.wsj.com/articles/trump-ordered-ukraine-ambassador-removed-after-complaints-from-giuliani-others-11570137147?shareToken=stb80f9f783f5541f89c4797fa9e5743aa" title="www.wsj.com">first broke the news</a>, which a senior administration official confirmed.</p></div></section></div><div class="remainder-content"><section><div><p class="font--body font-copy color-gray-darkest ma-0 pad-bottom-md undefined">Earlier Thursday, Trump called on China to investigate the younger Bidens business dealings abroad during the tenure of the former vice president.</p></div><div><p class="font--body font-copy color-gray-darkest ma-0 pad-bottom-md undefined">Trumps comments came as Democrats accelerated an impeachment inquiry that was sparked by a whistleblowers complaint that Trump had pressed Ukrainian President Volodymyr Zelensky for a similar investigation. Some Democrats said Trumps latest comments had generated another potential article of impeachment.</p></div><div><div class="cb bg-offwhite mt-xxs pad-top-md pad-bottom-md mb-lg ml-neg-gutter mr-neg-gutter mr-auto-ns ml-auto-ns db dn-ns relative" style="min-height:250px"><div class="absolute z-0" style="left:50%;top:50%">AD</div><div class="relative z-1"><div class=""><wp-ad class="hide-for-print hide-for-print" id="slug_mob_bigbox"></wp-ad></div></div></div></div><div><figure class="pad-top-xs mb-md ml-neg-gutter mr-neg-gutter mr-auto-ns ml-auto-ns center hide-for-print"><div class="powa-wrapper"><div class="powa-skip" data-ad-bar="1" data-aspect-ratio="0.5625" data-blurb="true" data-org="wapo" data-playthrough="true" data-uuid="4cd84996-f6b8-456b-a96a-fd9ac1b267f7"></div></div></figure></div><div><p class="font--body font-copy color-gray-darkest ma-0 pad-bottom-md undefined">As Trump spoke to reporters at the White House, Kurt D. Volker, who resigned last week as Trumps special envoy for Ukraine, was being interviewed behind closed doors in front of three House committees. Volker was among the officials mentioned by name in the whistleblowers complaint.</p></div><div><div class="cb bg-offwhite mt-xxs pad-top-md pad-bottom-md mb-lg ml-neg-gutter mr-neg-gutter mr-auto-ns Nancy Pelosi (D-Calif.) accused her Republican colleagues of being loyal to Trump and not the Constitution.</p></div><div><p class="font--body font-copy color-gray-darkest ma-0 pad-bottom-md undefined">Trump <a href="https://www.washingtonpost.com/world/national-security/trump-involved-pence-in-efforts-to-pressure-ukraines-leader-though-aides-say-vice-president-was-unaware-of-pursuit-of-dirt-on-bidens/2019/10/02/263aa9e2-e4a7-11e9-b403-f738899982d2_story.html?tid=lk_inline_manual_10">involved Vice President Pence in efforts to pressure Ukraines leader</a>, though officials say that Pence was unaware of allegations in the whistleblower complaint</p></div><div><p class="font--body font-copy color-gray-darkest ma-0 pad-bottom-md undefined">Odd markings, ellipses fuel <a of Trumps Ukraine call</p></div><div><figure class="pad-top-xs mb-md ml-neg-gutter mr-neg-gutter mr-auto-ns ml-auto-ns center hide-for-print"><div class="powa-wrapper"><div class="powa-skip" class="font--body font-copy color-gray-darkest ma-0 pad-bottom-md undefined"><b>7:20 p.m.: Volker concludes more than nine hours of testimony on Capitol Hill, Democrats say he provided evidence Trump used Biden investigation as contingency for meeting with Ukraine president</b></p></div><div><div class="cb bg-offwhite mt-xxs pad-top-md pad-bottom-md mb-lg ml-neg-gutter mr-neg-gutter mr-auto-ns ml-auto-ns dn db-ns relative" style="min-height:250px"><div class="absolute z-0" style="left:50%;top:50%">AD</div><div class="relative z-1"><div class=""><wp-ad class="hide-for-print hide-for-print" id="slug_inline_bb_2"></wp-ad></div></div></div></div><div><p class="font--body font-copy color-gray-darkest ma-0 pad-bottom-md undefined">The former special envoy for Ukraine spoke to congressional investigators all day, offering them insights into the White Houses efforts to get Ukraine to dig up information about Joe and Hunter Biden.</p></div><div><div class="cb bg-offwhite mt-xxs pad-top-md pad-bottom-md mb-lg ml-neg-gutter mr-neg-gutter mr-auto-ns ml-auto-ns db dn-ns relative" style="min-height:250px"><div class="absolute z-0" style="left:50%;top:50%">AD</div><div class="relative z-1"><div class=""><wp-ad class="hide-for-print hide-for-print" id="slug_mob_bigbox_3"></wp-ad></div></div></div></div><div><p class="font--body font-copy color-gray-darkest ma-0 pad-bottom-md undefined">Leaving the meeting, Rep. Eric Swalwell (D-Calif.) said Volker had provided evidence that a meeting Trump promised Ukraine President Zelensky was contingent on the country investigating Biden.</p></div><div><p class="font--body font-copy color-gray-darkest ma-0 pad-bottom-md undefined">We will be providing evidence very shortly that characterizes that for Zelensky to get a meeting with Trump, that Zelensky had to one, investigate the 2016 election, essentially go back and exonerate Russias role, and two, that Zelensky would have to investigate Biden. That was an understood predicate for the meeting, Swalwell said.</p></div><div><p class="font--body font-copy color-gray-darkest ma-0 pad-bottom-md undefined">Swalwell said there is also evidence that a State Department official was concerned that security assistance [to Ukraine] is being held back because of a domestic political campaign.</p></div><div><div class="cb bg-offwhite mt-xxs pad-top-md pad-bottom-md mb-lg ml-neg-gutter mr-neg-gutter mr-auto-ns ml-auto-ns dn db-ns relative" style="min-height:250px"><div class="absolute z-0" style="left:50%;top:50%">AD</div><div class="relative z-1"><div class=""><wp-ad class="hide-for-print hide-for-print" id="slug_inline_bb_3"></wp-ad></div></div></div></div><div><div class="cb bg-offwhite mt-xxs pad-top-md pad-bottom-md mb-lg ml-neg-gutter mr-neg-gutter mr-auto-ns ml-auto-ns db dn-ns relative" style="min-height:250px"><div class="absolute z-0" style="left:50%;top:50%">AD</div><div class="relative z-1"><div class=""><wp-ad class="hide-for-print hide-for-print" id="slug_mob_bigbox_4"></wp-ad></div></div></div></div><div><p class="font--body font-copy color-gray-darkest ma-0 pad-bottom-md undefined">Earlier, Volker told the committees that hed warned Giuliani not to trust incriminating information about Biden coming from Ukraine. He also told lawmakers that he and other State Department officials warned the Ukrainians not to involve themselves in U.S. politics because it could hurt them long-term.</p></div><div><p class="font--body font-copy color-gray-darkest ma-0 pad-bottom-md undefined"><i> Rachael Bade </i></p></div><div><div><div><hr style="margin-top:-10px;margin-bottom:-10px;"/></div></div></div><div><p class="font--body font-copy color-gray-darkest ma-0 pad-bottom-md undefined"><b>5:45 p.m.: Trump reportedly ordered U.S. ambassador to Ukraine replaced over complaints she was obstructing Biden investigation</b></p></div><div><p class="font--body font-copy color-gray-darkest ma-0 pad-bottom-md undefined">Trump ordered the removal of U.S. ambassador Marie Yovanovitch from her post in Kiev after hearing concerns from Giuliani and former Texas congressman Pete Sessions, among others, according to a senior administration official, who confirmed the Wall Street Journals reporting.</p></div><div><div class="cb bg-offwhite mt-xxs pad-top-md pad-bottom-md mb-lg ml-neg-gutter mr-neg-gutter mr-auto-ns ml-auto-ns db dn-ns relative" style="min-height:250px"><div class="absolute z-0" style="left:50%;top:50%">AD</div><div class="relative z-1"><div class=""><wp-ad class="hide-for-print hide-for-print" id="slug_mob_bigbox_5"></wp-ad></div></div></div></div><div><p class="font--body font-copy color-gray-darkest ma-0 pad-bottom-md undefined">Giuliani informed the president that he thought Yovanovitch was blocking his investigation into Biden and that she was against Trump. Sessions, in 2018 when he was still in office, reportedly asked for her removal because hed heard she had a bias against Trump.</p></div><div><div class="cb bg-offwhite mt-xxs pad-top-md pad-bottom-md mb-lg ml-neg-gutter mr-neg-gutter mr-auto-ns ml-auto-ns dn db-ns relative" style="min-height:250px"><div class="absolute z-0" style="left:50%;top:50%">AD</div><div class="relative z-1"><div class=""><wp-ad class="hide-for-print hide-for-print" id="slug_inline_bb_4"></wp-ad></div></div></div></div><div><p class="font--body font-copy color-gray-darkest ma-0 pad-bottom-md undefined">Trump said that he wanted it done quickly, the senior administration official said. Yovanovitch, who Trump disparaged on his call with the Ukrainian president in July, was called home in spring before her post ended.</p></div><div><p class="font--body font-copy color-gray-darkest ma-0 pad-bottom-md undefined">Giuliani has repeatedly criticized the ambassador and the embassy to The Post and others. He told the Journal, which <a href="https://www.wsj.com/articles/trump-ordered-ukraine-ambassador-removed-after-complaints-from-giuliani-others-11570137147" title="www.wsj.com">first broke</a> the story, that he had seen Yovanovitch as an obstacle in his pursuit for information about Biden from Ukrainians.</p></div><div><div class="cb bg-offwhite mt-xxs pad-top-md pad-bottom-md mb-lg ml-neg-gutter mr-neg-gutter mr-auto-ns ml-auto-ns db dn-ns relative" style="min-height:250px"><div class="absolute z-0" style="left:50%;top:50%">AD</div><div class="relative z-1"><div class=""><wp-ad class="hide-for-print hide-for-print" id="slug_mob_bigbox_6"></wp-ad></div></div></div></div><div><p class="font--body font-copy color-gray-darkest ma-0 pad-bottom-md undefined">Giuliani said in an interview Thursday that he had repeatedly pushed for the ambassador to be fired and the president agreed. But it was not carried out for some time, he said.</p></div><div><p class="font--body font-copy color-gray-darkest ma-0 pad-bottom-md undefined">The state department was trying to protect her, he said. They are also discussing whether to make it public.</p></div><div><p class="font--body font-copy color-gray-darkest ma-0 pad-bottom-md undefined">The details of the IRS complaint follow news of a separate, explosive whistleblower complaint filed in August by a member of the intelligence community. Rob Portman (Ohio), Ron Johnson (Wis.), and Mark Kirk (Ill.) and sent to Ukraines then-president Petro Poroshenko, asks him to make changes in the office of the top prosecutor.</p></div><div><p class="font--body font-copy color-gray-darkest ma-0 pad-bottom-md undefined">The letter, first unearthed by CNN, shows that then-vice president Joe Biden was not alone in wanting Ukraine to oust its prosecutor over concerns about the corruption pervasive in the country.</p></div><div><p class="font--body font-copy color-gray-darkest ma-0 pad-bottom-md undefined">The senators wrote to the Ukrainian president that they urge you to press ahead with urgent reforms to the Prosecutor Generals office and judiciary.</p></div><div><p class="font--body font-copy color-gray-darkest ma-0 pad-bottom-md undefined">Trump has said that Biden wanted the prosecutor ousted because hed investigated a Ukrainian natural gas company that employed Bidens son, Hunter. But in his remarks here, Biden slammed the GOP and hatchet men who he said echo Trumps words.</p></div><div><p class="font--body font-copy color-gray-darkest ma-0 pad-bottom-md undefined">He is repeatedly smearing me and my family. His party fans out to carry the smear, Biden said.</p></div><div><p class="font--body font-copy color-gray-darkest ma-0 pad-bottom-md undefined">Read more <a href="https://www.washingtonpost.com/politics/biden-in-fiery-remarks-tells-trump-im-not-going-anywhere/2019/10/02/4d2f88d4-e56e-11e9-a6e8-8759c5c7f608_story.html?tid=lk_inline_manual_245">here</a>.</p></div><div><p class="font--body font-copy color-gray-darkest ma-0 pad-bottom-md undefined"><i> Cleve R. Wootson Jr. and Colby Itkowitz</i></p></div><div><div><div><hr style="margin-top:-10px;margin-bottom:-10px;"/></div></div></div><div><p class="font--body font-copy color-gray-darkest ma-0 pad-bottom-md undefined"><b>6 a.m.: Whistleblower drafted complaint entirely on their own, lawyer says</b></p></div><div><p class="font--body font-copy color-gray-darkest ma-0 pad-bottom-md undefined">A lawyer for the whistleblower said Wednesday that the whistleblower drafted the complaint entirely on their own and without input of Congress.</p></div><div><p class="font--body font-copy color-gray-darkest ma-0 pad-bottom-md undefined">The statement came after Trump, at a joint news conference with Finnish President Sauli Niinist, accused Schiff, with no evidence, of having helped write the complaint.</p></div><div><p class="font--body font-copy color-gray-darkest ma-0 pad-bottom-md undefined">Trump made the comment in response to a question about a New York Times report stating that Schiff had learned the outlines of the whistleblowers concerns days before the individual filed a formal complaint.</p></div><div><p class="font--body font-copy color-gray-darkest ma-0 pad-bottom-md undefined">The Whistleblower drafted the Complaint entirely on their own, Mark Zaid, a lawyer for the whistleblower, said in a statement. In fact, none of the legal team saw the Complaint until it was publicly released by Congress. To be unequivocally clear, no Member or congressional staff had any input into or reviewed the Complaint before it was submitted to the Intelligence Community Inspector General.</p></div></section></div></div><div class="mb-lg pad-bottom-xs pad-top-xs" data-qa="comments-btn"><div class="comments btn btn-white db hide-for-print"><a class="gray-darkest hover-inherit
